					&lt;/div&gt;

							&lt;% if ( sponsor.sponsor_type == 1 ) { %&gt;
								&lt;span class="module-story--sponsor link-txt"&gt;Cosmopolitan + &lt;%= sponsor.sponsor_name %&gt;&lt;span&gt;
							&lt;% } else if ( sponsor.sponsor_type == 3 ) { %&gt;
								&lt;span class="module-story--sponsor link-txt"&gt;Provided by &lt;%= sponsor.sponsor_name %&gt;&lt;/span&gt;
